Subject: [dm-l] Digital Networking Even - Queen Mary, University of London,	21

Dear Digital Medievalists,

Registration is now open for a Digital Networking event at Queen Mary,
University of London.  Supported by the British Academy, the day will bring
together early career scholars interested in developing Digital Humanities
projects. It will combine targeted networking sessions and group workshops,
with presentations by guest speakers designed to address the practicalities
of running digital projects and to provide advice on grant applications.
 For more details see the attached PDF, and circulate widely!

Best

Eyal

Dr Eyal Poleg

Lecturer in Material History
School of History
Queen Mary University of London

_redacted_(a)qmul.ac.uk
